   <script>
   /* CSS rel=preload polyfill. Depends on loadCSS function. [c]2016 @scottjehl, Filament Group, Inc. Licensed MIT  */
(function (w) {
   // rel=preload support test
   if (!w.loadCSS) {
      return;
   }
   var rp = loadCSS.relpreload = {};
   rp.support = function () {
      try {
         return w.document.createElement("link").relList.supports("preload");
      } catch (e) {
         return false;
      }
   };

   // loop preload links and fetch using loadCSS
   rp.poly = function () {
      var links = w.document.getElementsByTagName("link");
      for (var i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
         var link = links[i];
         if (link.rel === "preload" && link.getAttribute("as") === "style") {
            w.loadCSS(link.href, link);
            link.rel = null;
         }
      }
   };

   // if link[rel=preload] is not supported, we must fetch the CSS manually using loadCSS
   if (!rp.support()) {
      rp.poly();
      var run = w.setInterval(rp.poly, 300);
      if (w.addEventListener) {
         w.addEventListener("load", function () {
            w.clearInterval(run);
         });
      }
      if (w.attachEvent) {
         w.attachEvent("onload", function () {
            w.clearInterval(run);
         })
      }
   }
}(this));</script>

                  <script>
                     $(document).ready(function () {
                        $('.jq-search-job-request-filter').click(function () {
                           var form = $('#quick-search-form'),
                              params = form.serializeArray().filter(function (item) {
                                 //Filter empty parameters
                                 return !!item.value.length;
                              }).map(function (item) {
                                 if (item.name === "priceTo" && isNaN(item.value)) {
                                    item.value = -1;
                                 }
                                 else {
                                    item.value = encodeURIComponent(item.value);
                                 }

                                 return item;
                              });

                           params = $.param(params);

                           c24.colorbox.createJsonp("https://www.chrono24.com/user/create-searchtask.htm?suppressMobile=1&searchQueryString=" + encodeURIComponent(params), {size: "md"});
                        });
                     });
                  </script>
                     <button type="submit" name="submit" class="btn btn-primary pull-right">Show results</button>
                  <span class="cancel btn btn-text m-r-4 pull-right">Cancel</span>
               </div>
            </div>
         </div>
      </div>
      <script>
            var filterHandler;

            function toggleSelectedFiltersBar() {
               var selectedFiltersBar = $('#selected-filters-bar');
               selectedFiltersBar.height(selectedFiltersBar[0].scrollHeight);
               $('#jq-selected-filters').toggleClass('closed');
               selectedFiltersBar.toggleClass('closed');
            }

            function initFilters() {
               filterHandler = new c24.filterHandler({
                  priceCurrencySign: '$',
                  priceFromLabel: 'from {0}',
                  priceToLabel: 'to {0}',
                  gaTrackingLabel: 'search.wristwatch',
                  stickyFilterStopContainer: $("#jq-sticky-stopper")
               });

               
               var selectedFiltersBar = $('#selected-filters-bar');
               if (selectedFiltersBar.length > 0) {
                  var selecedFiltersHeight = selectedFiltersBar[0].scrollHeight;
                  if (selecedFiltersHeight > 40) $("#jq-filterbar-toggle").show();
               }
            }

            $(document).ready(function () {
               initFilters();
            });

            function removeFilter(fg, value) {
               if (filterHandler == null) {
                  setTimeout(function () {
                     removeFilter(fg, value);
                  }, 100);

                  return;
               }

               if (value.length == 0) {
                  filterHandler.removeAllSelectedFilters(fg, false);
               } else {
                  filterHandler.removeSelectedFilter(fg, value, false);
               }

               $("#quick-search-form").submit();
            }

            // Filter Tracking in Plain JS, so it can be pushed before GTM
            var tempCategory = "";
            var tempData = [];
            var data = {};
            var formElements = document.forms["quick-search-form"];
            for (var i = 0; i < formElements.length; i++) {
               if (!formElements.elements[i].checked) continue;

               if (formElements.elements[i].name != tempCategory) {
                  if (tempCategory != "") {
                     data[tempCategory] = tempData;
                  }
                  tempData = [];
                  tempCategory = formElements.elements[i].name;
               }

               if (tempCategory == 'manufacturerIds' || tempCategory == 'models') {
                  tempData.push(formElements.elements[i].getAttribute('data-label'));
               } else {
                  tempData.push(formElements.elements[i].value);
               }
            }
            data[tempCategory] = tempData;

            var priceFrom = document.getElementById("jq-price-from");
            if (priceFrom.value > 0) data['priceFrom'] = priceFrom.value;

            var priceTo = document.getElementById("jq-price-to");
            if (priceTo.value > 0) data['priceTo'] = priceTo.value;

            dataLayer.push(data);
         </script>

   <script>
      $(document).ready(function() {
         $('select.result-sorting').on('change', function() {
            var selectedOption = $(this).find("option:selected").data("tce-action");
            tce('search.wristwatch', selectedOption);
            
               if( selectedOption.indexOf("price") !== -1 ) {
                  var logEvent = selectedOption.indexOf("price-desc") !== -1 ? "price-desc" : "price-asc";
                  tvle(logEvent);
               } else if( selectedOption === "sortOrder: newest") {
                  tvle("sort.newest");
               }
            
            c24.tools.open($(this).val());
         });
      });
   </script></div>

                     <script>

                        var viewportHeight;
                        var zoneTop;
                        var zoneBottom;

                        var checkVisibility = function (element) {
                           var thisTop = $(element).offset().top - $(window).scrollTop();

                           if (thisTop >= zoneTop && (thisTop + $(element).height()) <= zoneBottom) {
                              return true; // inside of zone
                           } else {
                              return false; // outside of zone
                           }
                        }

                        $(document).ready(function () {
                           viewportHeight = $(window).height();
                           zoneTop = viewportHeight * .2;
                           zoneBottom = viewportHeight * .8;

                           $(window).on('scroll', function () {
                              $('div[data-crossselling] > div:first-child').each(function () {
                                 if (checkVisibility(this)) $(this).addClass('viewed');
                                 else $(this).removeClass('viewed');
                              });

                              $('div[data-crossselling] > div:last-child').each(function () {
                                 if (checkVisibility(this)) $(this).addClass('viewed');
                                 else $(this).removeClass('viewed');
                              });
                           });
                        });
                     </script>

         <script type="text/javascript">
      $(document).ready(function () {
         var hasSeenContactBox = c24.data.getString('97') === '1' || false,
            contactBox = $('#jq-contact-box'),
            contactBoxToggler = $('#jq-contact-box-toggle'),
            closeContactBox = $('.jq-close-contact-box'),
            userlikeIsOnPage = $('script[src*="userlike"]').length > 0;

         var isWebtest = 'false' === 'true';


         if (userlikeIsOnPage) {
            contactBoxToggler.remove();
            contactBox.remove();
            return;
         }
         contactBoxToggler.on('click.toggleContactBox', toggleContactBox);
         closeContactBox.on('click.toggleContactBox', toggleContactBox);


         function animateIn(element) {
            element.removeClass('box-out').addClass('box-in');
         }

         function animateOut(element) {
            element.removeClass('box-in').addClass('box-out')
         }

         function toggleContactBox() {
            if (!contactBox.hasClass('box-in')) {
               tce('sticky-widget-module', 'sticky-widget-maximize');
               animateOut(contactBoxToggler);
               animateIn(contactBox);
            }
            else {
               tce('sticky-widget-module', 'sticky-widget-minimize');
               animateIn(contactBoxToggler);
               animateOut(contactBox);
            }
         }

         if (!hasSeenContactBox && c24.meta.deviceCategory != 'mobile' && !isWebtest) {
            animateIn(contactBox);

            c24.layer.show(function () {
               var firstVisitorAnimation = setTimeout(function() {
                  animateIn(contactBoxToggler);
                  animateOut(contactBox);
               }, 10000);

               closeContactBox.one('click.cancelFirstVisitorAnimation', function() {
                  clearTimeout(firstVisitorAnimation);
               });

               c24.data.setString('97', '1', 31536000);
            }, 1300);
         } else {
            contactBoxToggler.addClass('box-static-in');
         }
      });
   </script>

<script>
   $(document).ready(function () {
      var cookieName = '18';

      
      if (c24.data.getString(cookieName) !== null) return;

      
      var supportPhoneNumber = $('.jq-us-support-phone-number'),
         closeIcon = $('.jq-close-us-support-phone-number'),
         isTransparent = true,
         delaySeconds = 15,
         showAgainAfterHours = 24;

      
      function showSupportPhoneNumber() {
         if (isTransparent) {
            supportPhoneNumber.addClass('transparent');
         }

         supportPhoneNumber.fadeIn('fast', function () {
            supportPhoneNumber.removeClass('hide-simple');
         });
      }

      
      function closeSupportPhoneNumber() {
         supportPhoneNumber.fadeOut('fast', function () {
            supportPhoneNumber.remove();
            c24.data.setString(cookieName, '1', showAgainAfterHours*60*60);
         });
      }

      
      function stickSupportPhoneNumber(direction) {
         if (direction !== 'down') {
            supportPhoneNumber.addClass('sticky');

            if (isTransparent) supportPhoneNumber.addClass('transparent');
         }
      }

      
      function dockSupportPhoneNumber(direction) {
         supportPhoneNumber.removeClass('sticky');

         if (isTransparent) supportPhoneNumber.removeClass('transparent');
      }

      
      setTimeout(showSupportPhoneNumber, delaySeconds * 1000);

      
      closeIcon.click(closeSupportPhoneNumber);

      
      var isVisible = new Waypoint.Inview({
         element: $('.footer'),
         entered: dockSupportPhoneNumber,
         enter: dockSupportPhoneNumber,
         exit: stickSupportPhoneNumber,
         exited: stickSupportPhoneNumber
      });
   });
</script><div class="footer inverted">
